[30;1m276 | [0m[35mthe moment, assume the tree isn't empty (we'll get back to that later).[0m

[30;1m109 | [0m[35m- Fix the C implementation to match the Python implementation and[0m
[30;1m110 | [0m[35m  allow setting custom node sizes for an entire application directly[0m
[30;1m111 | [0m[35m  by changing ``BTree.max_leaf_size`` and ``BTree.max_internal_size``[0m
[30;1m112 | [0m[35m  attributes, without having to create a new subclass. These[0m
[30;1m113 | [0m[35m  attributes can now also be read from the classes in the C[0m
